 pradhan nyaayadhish altamas kabir ke netritv vaali peeth ne kaha ki aaropee marine- macimiliano lator or salvator giron 24 or 25 farvari ko ho rahe chunaav main matdaan karne ke liye bharat main italy ke rajdoot ke nigaraanee or hiraasat ke tahat swadesh jaaenge

 peeth ne donon marinon or italy sarkaar ke is aavedan ke sweekaar kar liya ki unhen chaar hafte ke liye italy jane kii anumati pradaan kii jaae

 The Kargil War took place between India and Pakistan in 1999
 is yuddh ke kaaran ko jaanane se pehle bharat or pakistan kii bhugolic avasthiti ko jaananaa jaruri he
 The Line of Control between India and Pakistan is 740 kilometers long, which passes between mountains and inaccessible areas
 niyantran rekha par aksar tanaav kii sthitidonon deshon ke bich maujuuda niyantran rekha lagbhag waisi hi he, jaisi ki 1947 ke yuddh ke samay thi
 There was again a war between the two countries in 1965, in which Pakistan was badly defeated
 iske baad 1971 main ek baar phir yuddh hua
 In this war, East Pakistan broke up and became Bangladesh
 us samay bhi kashmir main kai jagahon par ladaai hui or niyantran rekha par donon deshon ne ek-duusare kii chaukiyon par niyantran kiya
 But tension has increased more along the Line of Control for the last decade and a half
 saath hi seemaa par ghuspaith main bhi ijapha hua he
 The Pakistan army engaged in helping the infiltrators under the same circumstances fought the Kargil War in May and July in 1999
 kai reporton se yah baat sabit ho chuki he ki pakistan kii sena ghuspaithiye aatankiyon kii bharat kii seemaa main ghusane main madad kar rahi thi

 The honor of this war was spared by the Pakistan Army
 The purpose of the Pakistan Army was to cross the Line of Control and seize important peaks of India

 yah yuddh 2 maah se bhi zyada samay tak chalaa tha
